Header not set\")\n   365→\t\treturn req\n   366→\t}\n   367→\n   368→\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n   369→\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n   370→\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n   371→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. Header not set\")\n   372→\t} else if len(tenantids) > 1 {\n   373→\t\t// Loki supports multiple tenant IDs, but we should receive them from different contexts\n   374→\t\tlogger.Error(strconv.Itoa(len(tenantids)) + \" tenant IDs found. Header not set\")\n   375→\t} else {\n   376→\t\treq.Header.Add(\"X-Scope-OrgID\", tenantids[0])\n   377→\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID \" + tenantids[0] + \" added to Loki request\")\n   378→\t}\n   379→\treturn req\n   380→}\n   381→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. 656→\n   657→// DecodeHTTPGrpcResponse decodes an httpgrp.HTTPResponse to queryrangebase.Response.\n   658→func (Codec) DecodeHTTPGrpcResponse(r *httpgrpc.HTTPResponse, req queryrangebase.Request) (queryrangebase.Response, error) {\n   659→\tif r.Code/100 != 2 {\n   660→\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(int(r.Code), \"%s\", string(r.Body))\n   661→\t}\n   662→\n   663→\theaders := 669→\n   670→func (Codec) EncodeHTTPGrpcResponse(_ context.Context, req *httpgrpc.HTTPRequest, res queryrangebase.Response) (*httpgrpc.HTTPResponse, error) {\n   671→\tversion := loghttp.GetVersion(req.Url)\n   672→\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n   673→\n   674→\tencodingFlags := httpreq.ExtractEncodingFlagsFromProto(req)\n   675→\n   676→\terr := encodeResponseJSONTo(version, res, 695→\n   696→func (c Codec) EncodeRequest(ctx context.Context, r queryrangebase.Request) (*http.Request, error) {\n   697→\theader := make(http.Header)\n   698→\n   699→\t// Add query tags\n 1415→func (Codec) MergeResponse(responses ...queryrangebase.Response) (queryrangebase.Response, error) {\n  1416→\tif len(responses) == 0 {\n  1417→\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"merging responses requires at least one response\")\n  1418→\t}\n  1419→\tvar mergedStats stats.Result\n  1420→\tswitch res := responses[0].(type) {\n  1421→\t// LokiPromResponse type is used for both instant and range queries.\n  1422→\t// Meaning, values that are merged can be either vector or matrix types.\n  1423→\tcase *LokiPromResponse:\n  1424→\n  1425→\t\tcodec := queryrangebase.PrometheusCodecForRangeQueries\n  1426→\t\tif res.Response.Data.ResultType == model.ValVector.String() {\n  1427→\t\t\tcodec = queryrangebase.PrometheusCodecForInstantQueries\n 1445→\tcase *LokiSeriesResponse:\n  1446→\t\tlokiSeriesRes := responses[0].(*LokiSeriesResponse)\n  1447→\n  1448→\t\tvar lokiSeriesData []logproto.SeriesIdentifier\n  1449→\t\tuniqueSeries := make(map[uint64]struct{})\n  1450→\n  1451→\t\t// The buffers are used by `series.Hash`. They are allocated\n  1452→\t\t// outside of the method in order to reuse them for the next\n  1453→\t\t// iteration. This saves a lot of allocations.\n  1454→\t\t// 1KB is used for `b` after some experimentation. The\n  1455→\t\t// benchmarks are ~10% faster in comparison to no buffer with\n  1456→\t\t// little overhead. A run with 4MB should the same speedup but\n  1457→\t\t// much much more overhead.\n  1458→\t\tb := make([]byte, 0, 1024)\n  1459→\t\tvar key uint64\n  1460→\n  1461→\t\t// only unique series should be merged\n  1462→\t\tfor _, res := range responses {\n  1463→\t\t\tlokiResult := res.(*LokiSeriesResponse)\n  1464→\t\t\tmergedStats.MergeSplit(lokiResult.Statistics)\n  1465→\t\t\tfor _, series := range lokiResult.Data {\n  1466→\t\t\t\t// Use series hash as the key.\n  1467→\t\t\t\tkey = series.Hash(b)\n  1468→\n  1469→\t\t\t\t// TODO(karsten): There is a chance that the\n  1470→\t\t\t\t// keys match but not the labels due to hash\n  1471→\t\t\t\t// collision. Ideally there's an else block the\n  1472→\t\t\t\t// compares the series labels. However, that's\n  1473→\t\t\t\t// not trivial. Besides, instance.Series has the\n  1474→\t\t\t\t// same issue in its deduping logic.\n  1475→\t\t\t\tif _, ok := uniqueSeries[key]; !ok {\n  1476→\t\t\t\t\tlokiSeriesData = append(lokiSeriesData, series)\n  1477→\t\t\t\t\tuniqueSeries[key] = struct{}{}\n  1478→\t\t\t\t}\n  1479→\t\t\t}\n  1480→\t\t}\n  1481→\n  1482→\t\treturn &LokiSeriesResponse{\n  1483→\t\t\tStatus:     lokiSeriesRes.Status,\n  1484→\t\t\tVersion:    lokiSeriesRes.Version,\n  1485→\t\t\tData:       lokiSeriesData,\n  1486→\t\t\tHeaders:    lokiSeriesRes.Headers,\n  1487→\t\t\tStatistics: mergedStats,\n  1488→\t\t}, nil\n  1489→\tcase *LokiSeriesResponseView:\n  1490→\t\tv := &MergedSeriesResponseView{}\n  1491→\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n  1492→\t\t\tv.responses = 1502→\t\tlabelNameRes := responses[0].(*LokiLabelNamesResponse)\n  1503→\t\tuniqueNames := make(map[string]struct{})\n  1504→\t\tnames := []string{}\n  1505→\n  1506→\t\t// only unique name should be 1521→\t\t\tHeaders:    labelNameRes.Headers,\n  1522→\t\t\tData:       names,\n  1523→\t\t\tStatistics: mergedStats,\n  1524→\t\t}, nil\n  1525→\tcase *IndexStatsResponse:\n  1526→\t\theaders := 1541→\n  1542→\t\tresps := make([]*logproto.VolumeResponse, 0, len(responses))\n  1543→\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n  1544→\t\t\tresps = append(resps, r.(*VolumeResponse).Response)\n  1545→\t\t}\n  1546→\n  1547→\t\treturn &VolumeResponse{\n  1548→\t\t\tResponse: seriesvolume.Merge(resps, resp0.Response.Limit),\n  1549→\t\t\tHeaders:  headers,\n  1550→\t\t}, nil\n  1551→\tcase *DetectedFieldsResponse:\n  1552→\t\tresp0 := responses[0].(*DetectedFieldsResponse)\n  1553→\t\theaders := resp0.Headers\n  1554→\t\tlimit := resp0.Response.GetLimit()\n  1555→\n  1556→\t\tfields := []*logproto.DetectedField{}\n  1557→\t\tvalues := []string{}\n  1558→\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n  1559→\t\t\tfields = append(fields, r.(*DetectedFieldsResponse).Response.Fields...)\n  1560→\t\t\tvalues = append(values, r.(*DetectedFieldsResponse).Response.Values...)\n  1561→\t\t}\n  1562→\n  1563→\t\tmergedFields, err := detected.MergeFields(fields, limit)\n  1564→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1565→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n  1566→\t\t}\n  1567→\n  1568→\t\tmergedValues, err := detected.MergeValues(values, limit)\n  1569→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1570→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n  1571→\t\t}\n  1572→\n  1573→\t\treturn &DetectedFieldsResponse{\n  1574→\t\t\tResponse: &logproto.DetectedFieldsResponse{\n  1575→\t\t\t\tFields: mergedFields,\n  1576→\t\t\t\tValues: mergedValues,\n  1577→\t\t\t\tLimit:  limit,\n  1578→\t\t\t},\n  1579→\t\t\tHeaders: headers,\n  1580→\t\t}, nil\n  1581→\tcase *DetectedLabelsResponse:\n  1582→\t\tresp0 := responses[0].(*DetectedLabelsResponse)\n  1583→\t\theaders := resp0.Headers\n  1584→\t\tvar labels []*logproto.DetectedLabel\n  1585→\n  1586→\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n  1587→\t\t\tlabels = append(labels, 1592→\t\t}\n  1593→\n  1594→\t\treturn &DetectedLabelsResponse{\n  1595→\t\t\tResponse: &logproto.DetectedLabelsResponse{\n  1596→\t\t\t\tDetectedLabels: mergedLabels,\n  1597→\t\t\t},\n  1598→\t\t\tHeaders: headers,\n  1599→\t\t}, nil\n  1600→\tdefault:\n  1601→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown response type (%T) in merging responses\", responses[0])\n  1602→\t}\n  1603→}\n  1604→\n  1605→// mergeOrderedNonOverlappingStreams merges a set of ordered, nonoverlapping responses by concatenating matching streams then running them through a heap to pull out limit values\n  1606→func mergeOrderedNonOverlappingStreams(resps []*LokiResponse, limit uint32, direction logproto.Direction) []logproto.Stream {\n  1607→\tvar total int\n  1608→\n  1609→\t// turn resps -> map[labels] []entries\n  1610→\tgroups := make(map[string]*byDir)\n  1611→\tfor _, resp := range resps {\n  1612→\t\tfor _, stream := range resp.Data.Result {\n  1613→\t\t\ts, ok := groups[stream.Labels]\n  1614→\t\t\tif !ok {\n  1615→\t\t\t\ts = &byDir{\n  1616→\t\t\t\t\tdirection: direction,\n  1617→\t\t\t\t\tlabels:    stream.Labels,\n  1618→\t\t\t\t}\n  1619→\t\t\t\tgroups[stream.Labels] = s\n  1620→\t\t\t}\n  1621→\n  1622→\t\t\ts.markers = append(s.markers, stream.Entries)\n  1623→\t\t\ttotal += len(stream.Entries)\n  1624→\t\t}\n  1625→\n  1626→\t\t// optimization: since limit has been reached, no need to append entries from subsequent responses\n  1627→\t\tif total >= int(limit) {\n  1628→\t\t\tbreak\n  1629→\t\t}\n  1630→\t}\n  1631→\n  1632→\tkeys := make([]string, 0, len(groups))\n  1633→\tfor key := range groups {\n  1634→\t\tkeys = append(keys, key)\n  1635→\t}\n  1636→\tif direction == logproto.BACKWARD {\n  1637→\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse(sort.StringSlice(keys)))\n  1638→\t} else {\n  1639→\t\tsort.Strings(keys)\n  1640→\t}\n  1641→\n  1642→\t// escape hatch, can just return all the streams\n  1643→\tif total <= int(limit) {\n  1644→\t\tresults := make([]logproto.Stream, 0, len(keys))\n  1645→\t\tfor _, key := range keys {\n  1646→\t\t\tresults = append(results, logproto.Stream{\n  1647→\t\t\t\tLabels:  key,\n  1648→\t\t\t\tEntries: groups[key].merge(),\n  1649→\t\t\t})\n  1650→\t\t}\n  1651→\t\treturn results\n  1652→\t}\n  1653→\n  1654→\tpq := &priorityqueue{\n  1655→\t\tdirection: direction,\n  1656→\t}\n  1657→\n  1658→\tfor _, key := range keys {\n  1659→\t\tstream := &logproto.Stream{\n  1660→\t\t\tLabels:  key,\n  1661→\t\t\tEntries: groups[key].merge(),\n  1662→\t\t}\n  1663→\t\tif len(stream.Entries) > 0 {\n  1664→\t\t\tpq.streams = append(pq.streams, stream)\n  1665→\t\t}\n  1666→\t}\n  1667→\n  1668→\theap.Init(pq)\n  1669→\n  1670→\tresultDict := make(map[string]*logproto.Stream)\n  1671→\n  1672→\t// we want the min(limit, num_entries)\n  1673→\tfor i := 0; i < int(limit) && pq.Len() > 0; i++ {\n  1674→\t\t// grab the next entry off the queue. This will be a stream (to preserve labels) with one entry.\n  1675→\t\tnext := heap.Pop(pq).(*logproto.Stream)\n  1676→\n  1677→\t\ts, ok := resultDict[next.Labels]\n  1678→\t\tif !ok {\n  1679→\t\t\ts = &logproto.Stream{\n  1680→\t\t\t\tLabels:  next.Labels,\n  1681→\t\t\t\tEntries: make([]logproto.Entry, 0, int(limit)/len(keys)), // allocation hack -- assume uniform distribution across labels\n  1682→\t\t\t}\n  1683→\t\t\tresultDict[next.Labels] = s\n  1684→\t\t}\n  1685→\t\t// TODO: make allocation friendly\n  1686→\t\ts.Entries = append(s.Entries, next.Entries...)\n  1687→\t}\n  1688→\n  1689→\tresults := make([]logproto.Stream, 0, len(resultDict))\n  1690→\tfor _, key := range keys {\n  1691→\t\tstream, ok := resultDict[key]\n  1692→\t\tif ok {\n  1693→\t\t\tresults = append(results, *stream)\n  1694→\t\t}\n  1695→\t}\n  1696→\n  1697→\treturn results\n  1698→}\n  1699→\n  1700→func toProtoMatrix(m loghttp.Matrix) []queryrangebase.SampleStream {\n  1701→\tres := make([]queryrangebase.SampleStream, 0, len(m))\n  1702→\n  1703→\tif len(m) == 0 {\n  1704→\t\treturn res\n  1705→\t}\n  1706→\n  1707→\tfor _, stream := range m {\n  1708→\t\tsamples := make([]logproto.LegacySample, 0, len(stream.Values))\n  1709→\t\tfor _, s := range stream.Values {\n  1710→\t\t\tsamples = append(samples, logproto.LegacySample{\n  1711→\t\t\t\tValue:       float64(s.Value),\n  1712→\t\t\t\tTimestampMs: int64(s.Timestamp),\n  1713→\t\t\t})\n  1714→\t\t}\n  1715→\t\tres = append(res, queryrangebase.SampleStream{\n  1716→\t\t\tLabels:  logproto.FromMetricsToLabelAdapters(stream.Metric),\n  1717→\t\t\tSamples: samples,\n  1718→\t\t})\n  1719→\t}\n  1720→\treturn res\n  1721→}\n  1722→\n  1723→func toProtoVector(v loghttp.Vector) []queryrangebase.SampleStream {\n  1724→\tres := make([]queryrangebase.SampleStream, 0, len(v))\n  1725→\n  1726→\tif len(v) == 0 {\n  1727→\t\treturn res\n  1728→\t}\n  1729→\tfor _, s := range v {\n  1730→\t\tres = append(res, queryrangebase.SampleStream{\n  1731→\t\t\tSamples: []logproto.LegacySample{{\n  1732→\t\t\t\tValue:       float64(s.Value),\n  1733→\t\t\t\tTimestampMs: int64(s.Timestamp),\n  1734→\t\t\t}},\n  1735→\t\t\tLabels: logproto.FromMetricsToLabelAdapters(s.Metric),\n  1736→\t\t})\n  1737→\t}\n  1738→\treturn res\n  1739→}\n  1740→\n  1741→func toProtoScalar(v loghttp.Scalar) []queryrangebase.SampleStream {\n  1742→\tres := make([]queryrangebase.SampleStream, 0, 1)\n  1743→\n  1744→\tres = append(res, queryrangebase.SampleStream{\n  1745→\t\tSamples: []logproto.LegacySample{{\n  1746→\t\t\tValue:       float64(v.Value),\n  1747→\t\t\tTimestampMs: v.Timestamp.UnixNano() / 1e6,\n  1748→\t\t}},\n  1749→\t\tLabels: nil,\n  1750→\t})\n  1751→\treturn res\n  1752→}\n  1753→\n  1754→func (res LokiResponse) Count() int64 {\n  1755→\tvar result int64\n  1756→\tfor _, s := range res.Data.Result {\n  1757→\t\tresult += int64(len(s.Entries))\n  1758→\t}\n  1759→\treturn result\n  1760→}\n  1761→\n  1762→func ParamsFromRequest(req queryrangebase.Request) (logql.Params, error) {\n  1763→\tswitch r := req.(type) {\n 0 {\n  2178→\t\treturn nil\n  2179→\t}\n  2180→\tvar (\n  2181→\t\tlokiRes       = responses[0].(*LokiResponse)\n  2182→\t\tmergedStats   stats.Result\n  2183→\t\tlokiResponses = make([]*LokiResponse, 0, len(responses))\n  2184→\t)\n  2185→\n  2186→\tuniqueWarnings := map[string]struct{}{}\n  2187→\tfor _, res := range responses {\n  2188→\t\tlokiResult := res.(*LokiResponse)\n  2189→\t\tmergedStats.MergeSplit(lokiResult.Statistics)\n  2190→\t\tlokiResponses = append(lokiResponses, lokiResult)\n  2191→\n  2192→\t\tfor _, w := range lokiResult.Warnings {\n  2193→\t\t\tuniqueWarnings[w] = struct{}{}\n  2194→\t\t}\n  2195→\t}\n  2196→\n  2197→\twarnings := maps.Keys(uniqueWarnings)\n  2198→\tsort.Strings(warnings)\n  2199→\n  2200→\tif len(warnings) == 0 {\n  2201→\t\t// When there are no warnings, keep it nil so it can be compared against\n  2202→\t\t// the default value\n  2203→\t\twarnings = nil\n  2204→\t}\n  2205→\n  2206→\treturn &LokiResponse{\n  2207→\t\tStatus:     loghttp.QueryStatusSuccess,\n  2208→\t\tDirection:  lokiRes.Direction,\n  2209→\t\tLimit:      lokiRes.Limit,\n  2210→\t\tVersion:    lokiRes.Version,\n  2211→\t\tErrorType:  lokiRes.ErrorType,\n  2212→\t\tError:      lokiRes.Error,\n  2213→\t\tStatistics: mergedStats,\n  2214→\t\tWarnings:   warnings,\n  2215→\t\tData: LokiData{\n  2216→\t\t\tResultType: loghttp.ResultTypeStream,\n  2217→\t\t\tResult:     mergeOrderedNonOverlappingStreams(lokiResponses, lokiRes.Limit, lokiRes.Direction),\n  2218→\t\t},\n  2219→\t}\n  2220→}\n  2221→\n  2222→func parseRangeQuery(r *http.Request) (*LokiRequest, error) {\n  2223→\trangeQuery, err := loghttp.ParseRangeQuery(r)\n  2224→\tif err != nil {\n  2225→\t\treturn nil, err\n  2226→\t}\n 2284→\n  2285→// escape hatch for including store chunks in the request\n  2286→func parseStoreChunks(r *http.Request) (*logproto.ChunkRefGroup, error) {\n  2287→\tif s := r.Form.Get(\"storeChunks\"); httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers),\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *DetectedFieldsRequest:\n\t\tvar resp logproto.DetectedFieldsResponse\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(buf, &resp); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"error decoding response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn &DetectedFieldsResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: &resp,\n\t\t\tHeaders:  httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers),\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *logproto.QueryPatternsRequest:\n\t\tvar resp logproto.QueryPatternsResponse\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(buf, &resp); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"error decoding response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn &QueryPatternsResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: &resp,\n\t\t\tHeaders:  httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers),\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *DetectedLabelsRequest:\n\t\tvar resp logproto.DetectedLabelsResponse\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(buf, &resp); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"error decoding response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn &DetectedLabelsResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: &resp,\n\t\t\tHeaders:  httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers),\n\t\t}, nil\n\tdefault:\n\t\tvar resp loghttp.QueryResponse\n\t\tif err := resp.UnmarshalJSON(buf); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"error decoding response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch string(resp.Data.ResultType) {\n\t\tcase loghttp.ResultTypeMatrix:\n\t\t\treturn &LokiPromResponse{\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &queryrangebase.PrometheusResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tStatus: resp.Status,\n\t\t\t\t\tData: queryrangebase.PrometheusData{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tResultType: loghttp.ResultTypeMatrix,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tResult:     toProtoMatrix(resp.Data.Result.(loghttp.Matrix)),\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\tHeaders:  convertPrometheusResponseHeadersToPointers(httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers)),\n\t\t\t\t\tWarnings: resp.Warnings,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tStatistics: resp.Data.Statistics,\n\t\t\t}, nil\n\t\tcase loghttp.ResultTypeStream:\n\t\t\t// This is the same as in querysharding.go\n\t\t\tparams, err := ParamsFromRequest(req)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar path string\n\t\t\tswitch r := req.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *LokiRequest:\n\t\t\t\tpath = r.GetPath()\n\t\t\tcase *LokiInstantRequest:\n\t\t\t\tpath = r.GetPath()\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"expected *LokiRequest or *LokiInstantRequest, got (%T)\", r)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn &LokiResponse{\n\t\t\t\tStatus:     resp.Status,\n\t\t\t\tDirection:  params.Direction(),\n\t\t\t\tLimit:      params.Limit(),\n\t\t\t\tVersion:    uint32(loghttp.GetVersion(path)),\n\t\t\t\tStatistics: resp.Data.Statistics,\n\t\t\t\tData: LokiData{\n\t\t\t\t\tResultType: loghttp.ResultTypeStream,\n\t\t\t\t\tResult:     resp.Data.Result.(loghttp.Streams).ToProto(),\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tHeaders:  httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers),\n\t\t\t\tWarnings: resp.Warnings,\n\t\t\t}, nil\n\t\tcase loghttp.ResultTypeVector:\n\t\t\treturn &LokiPromResponse{\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &queryrangebase.PrometheusResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tStatus: resp.Status,\n\t\t\t\t\tData: queryrangebase.PrometheusData{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tResultType: loghttp.ResultTypeVector,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tResult:     toProtoVector(resp.Data.Result.(loghttp.Vector)),\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\tHeaders:  convertPrometheusResponseHeadersToPointers(httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers)),\n\t\t\t\t\tWarnings: resp.Warnings,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tStatistics: resp.Data.Statistics,\n\t\t\t}, nil\n\t\tcase loghttp.ResultTypeScalar:\n\t\t\treturn &LokiPromResponse{\n\t\t\t\tResponse: &queryrangebase.PrometheusResponse{\n\t\t\t\t\tStatus: resp.Status,\n\t\t\t\t\tData: queryrangebase.PrometheusData{\n\t\t\t\t\t\tResultType: loghttp.ResultTypeScalar,\n\t\t\t\t\t\tResult:     toProtoScalar(resp.Data.Result.(loghttp.Scalar)),\n\t\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\tHeaders:  convertPrometheusResponseHeadersToPointers(httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(headers)),\n\t\t\t\t\tWarnings: resp.Warnings,\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\tStatistics: resp.Data.Statistics,\n\t\t\t}, nil\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"unsupported response type, got (%s)\", string(resp.Data.ResultType))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc decodeResponseProtobuf(r *http.Response, req queryrangebase.Request) (queryrangebase.Response, error) {\n\tvar buf []byte\n\tvar err error\n\tif buffer, ok := r.Body.(Buffer); ok {\n\t\tbuf = buffer.Bytes()\n\t} else {\n\t\tbuf, err = io.ReadAll(r.Body)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"error decoding response: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Shortcut series responses without deserialization.\n\tif _, ok := req.(*LokiSeriesRequest); ok {\n\t\treturn GetLokiSeriesResponseView(buf)\n\t}\n\n\tresp := &QueryResponse{}\n\terr = resp.Unmarshal(buf)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"error decoding response: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\theaders := httpResponseHeadersToPromResponseHeaders(r.Header)\n\tswitch req.(type) {\n\tcase *LokiSeriesRequest:\n\t\treturn resp.GetSeries().WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\tcase *LabelRequest:\n\t\treturn resp.GetLabels().WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\tcase *logproto.IndexStatsRequest:\n\t\treturn resp.GetStats().WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\tcase *logproto.ShardsRequest:\n\t\treturn resp.GetShardsResponse().WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\tdefault:\n\t\tswitch concrete := resp.Response.(type) {\n\t\tcase *QueryResponse_Prom:\n\t\t\treturn concrete.Prom.WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\t\tcase *QueryResponse_Streams:\n\t\t\treturn concrete.Streams.WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\t\tcase *QueryResponse_TopkSketches:\n\t\t\treturn concrete.TopkSketches.WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\t\tcase *QueryResponse_QuantileSketches:\n\t\t\treturn concrete.QuantileSketches.WithHeaders(headers), nil\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"unsupported response type, got (%T)\", resp.Response)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (Codec) EncodeResponse(ctx context.Context, req *http.Request, res queryrangebase.Response) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tif req.Header.Get(\"Accept\") == ProtobufType {\n\t\treturn encodeResponseProtobuf(ctx, res)\n\t}\n\n\t// Default to JSON.\n\tversion := loghttp.GetVersion(req.RequestURI)\n\tencodingFlags := httpreq.ExtractEncodingFlags(req)\n\treturn encodeResponseJSON(ctx, version, res, encodingFlags)\n}\n\nfunc encodeResponseJSON(ctx context.Context, version loghttp.Version, res queryrangebase.Response, encodeFlags httpreq.EncodingFlags) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tsp, _ := opentracing.StartSpanFromContext(ctx, \"codec.EncodeResponse\")\n\tdefer sp.Finish()\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\terr := encodeResponseJSONTo(version, res, &buf, encodeFlags)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tsp.LogFields(otlog.Int(\"bytes\", buf.Len()))\n\n\tresp := http.Response{\n\t\tHeader: http.Header{\n\t\t\t\"Content-Type\": []string{\"application/json; charset=UTF-8\"},\n\t\t},\n\t\tBody:       io.NopCloser(&buf),\n\t\tStatusCode: http.StatusOK,\n\t}\n\treturn &resp, nil\n}\n\nfunc encodeResponseJSONTo(version loghttp.Version, res queryrangebase.Response, w io.Writer, encodeFlags httpreq.EncodingFlags) error {\n\tswitch response := res.(type) {\n\tcase *LokiPromResponse:\n\t\treturn response.encodeTo(w)\n\tcase *LokiResponse:\n\t\tstreams := make([]logproto.Stream, len(response.Data.Result))\n\n\t\tfor i, stream := range response.Data.Result {\n\t\t\tstreams[i] = logproto.Stream{\n\t\t\t\tLabels:  stream.Labels,\n\t\t\t\tEntries: stream.Entries,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif version == loghttp.VersionLegacy {\n\t\t\tresult := logqlmodel.Result{\n\t\t\t\tData:       logqlmodel.Streams(streams),\n\t\t\t\tStatistics: response.Statistics,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif err := marshal_legacy.WriteQueryResponseJSON(result, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tif err := marshal.WriteQueryResponseJSON(logqlmodel.Streams(streams), response.Warnings, response.Statistics, w, encodeFlags); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase *MergedSeriesResponseView:\n\t\tif err := WriteSeriesResponseViewJSON(response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *LokiSeriesResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteSeriesResponseJSON(response.Data, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *LokiLabelNamesResponse:\n\t\tif loghttp.Version(response.Version) == loghttp.VersionLegacy {\n\t\t\tif err := marshal_legacy.WriteLabelResponseJSON(logproto.LabelResponse{Values: response.Data}, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tif err := marshal.WriteLabelResponseJSON(response.Data, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase *IndexStatsResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteIndexStatsResponseJSON(response.Response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *ShardsResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteIndexShardsResponseJSON(response.Response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *VolumeResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteVolumeResponseJSON(response.Response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *DetectedFieldsResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteDetectedFieldsResponseJSON(response.Response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *QueryPatternsResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteQueryPatternsResponseJSON(response.Response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tcase *DetectedLabelsResponse:\n\t\tif err := marshal.WriteDetectedLabelsResponseJSON(response.Response, w); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"%s\", fmt.Sprintf(\"invalid response format, got (%T)\", res))\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc encodeResponseProtobuf(ctx context.Context, res queryrangebase.Response) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tsp, _ := opentracing.StartSpanFromContext(ctx, \"codec.EncodeResponse\")\n\tdefer sp.Finish()\n\n\tp, err := QueryResponseWrap(res)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, httpgrpc.Errorf(http.StatusInternalServerError, \"%s\", err.Error())\n\t}\n\n\tbuf, err := p.Marshal()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"could not marshal protobuf: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tresp := http.Response{\n\t\tHeader: http.Header{\n\t\t\t\"Content-Type\": []string{ProtobufType},\n\t\t},\n\t\tBody:       io.NopCloser(bytes.NewBuffer(buf)),\n\t\tStatusCode: http.StatusOK,\n\t}\n\treturn &resp, nil\n}\n\n// NOTE: When we would start caching response from non-metric queries we would have to consider cache gen headers as well in\n// MergeResponse implementation for Loki codecs same as it is done in Cortex at https://github.com/cortexproject/cortex/blob/21bad57b346c730d684d6d0205efef133422ab28/pkg/querier/queryrange/query_range.go#L170\nfunc (Codec) MergeResponse(responses ...queryrangebase.Response) (queryrangebase.Response, error) {\n\tif len(responses) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"merging responses requires at least one response\")\n\t}\n\tvar mergedStats stats.Result\n\tswitch res := responses[0].(type) {\n\t// LokiPromResponse type is used for both instant and range queries.\n\t// Meaning, values that are merged can be either vector or matrix types.\n\tcase *LokiPromResponse:\n\n\t\tcodec := queryrangebase.PrometheusCodecForRangeQueries\n\t\tif res.Response.Data.ResultType == model.ValVector.String() {\n\t\t\tcodec = queryrangebase.PrometheusCodecForInstantQueries\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tpromResponses := make([]queryrangebase.Response, 0, len(responses))\n\t\tfor _, res := range responses {\n\t\t\tmergedStats.MergeSplit(res.(*LokiPromResponse).Statistics)\n\t\t\tpromResponses = append(promResponses, res.(*LokiPromResponse).Response)\n\t\t}\n\t\tpromRes, err := codec.MergeResponse(promResponses...)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn &LokiPromResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse:   promRes.(*queryrangebase.PrometheusResponse),\n\t\t\tStatistics: mergedStats,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *LokiResponse:\n\t\treturn mergeLokiResponse(responses...), nil\n\tcase *LokiSeriesResponse:\n\t\tlokiSeriesRes := responses[0].(*LokiSeriesResponse)\n\n\t\tvar lokiSeriesData []logproto.SeriesIdentifier\n\t\tuniqueSeries := make(map[uint64]struct{})\n\n\t\t// The buffers are used by `series.Hash`. They are allocated\n\t\t// outside of the method in order to reuse them for the next\n\t\t// iteration. This saves a lot of allocations.\n\t\t// 1KB is used for `b` after some experimentation. The\n\t\t// benchmarks are ~10% faster in comparison to no buffer with\n\t\t// little overhead. A run with 4MB should the same speedup but\n\t\t// much much more overhead.\n\t\tb := make([]byte, 0, 1024)\n\t\tvar key uint64\n\n\t\t// only unique series should be merged\n\t\tfor _, res := range responses {\n\t\t\tlokiResult := res.(*LokiSeriesResponse)\n\t\t\tmergedStats.MergeSplit(lokiResult.Statistics)\n\t\t\tfor _, series := range lokiResult.Data {\n\t\t\t\t// Use series hash as the key.\n\t\t\t\tkey = series.Hash(b)\n\n\t\t\t\t// TODO(karsten): There is a chance that the\n\t\t\t\t// keys match but not the labels due to hash\n\t\t\t\t// collision. Ideally there's an else block the\n\t\t\t\t// compares the series labels. However, that's\n\t\t\t\t// not trivial. Besides, instance.Series has the\n\t\t\t\t// same issue in its deduping logic.\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := uniqueSeries[key]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tlokiSeriesData = append(lokiSeriesData, series)\n\t\t\t\t\tuniqueSeries[key] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &LokiSeriesResponse{\n\t\t\tStatus:     lokiSeriesRes.Status,\n\t\t\tVersion:    lokiSeriesRes.Version,\n\t\t\tData:       lokiSeriesData,\n\t\t\tHeaders:    lokiSeriesRes.Headers,\n\t\t\tStatistics: mergedStats,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *LokiSeriesResponseView:\n\t\tv := &MergedSeriesResponseView{}\n\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n\t\t\tv.responses = append(v.responses, r.(*LokiSeriesResponseView))\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn v, nil\n\tcase *MergedSeriesResponseView:\n\t\tv := &MergedSeriesResponseView{}\n\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n\t\t\tv.responses = append(v.responses, r.(*MergedSeriesResponseView).responses...)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn v, nil\n\tcase *LokiLabelNamesResponse:\n\t\tlabelNameRes := responses[0].(*LokiLabelNamesResponse)\n\t\tuniqueNames := make(map[string]struct{})\n\t\tnames := []string{}\n\n\t\t// only unique name should be merged\n\t\tfor _, res := range responses {\n\t\t\tlokiResult := res.(*LokiLabelNamesResponse)\n\t\t\tmergedStats.MergeSplit(lokiResult.Statistics)\n\t\t\tfor _, labelName := range lokiResult.Data {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := uniqueNames[labelName]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tnames = append(names, labelName)\n\t\t\t\t\tuniqueNames[labelName] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &LokiLabelNamesResponse{\n\t\t\tStatus:     labelNameRes.Status,\n\t\t\tVersion:    labelNameRes.Version,\n\t\t\tHeaders:    labelNameRes.Headers,\n\t\t\tData:       names,\n\t\t\tStatistics: mergedStats,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *IndexStatsResponse:\n\t\theaders := responses[0].(*IndexStatsResponse).Headers\n\t\tstats := make([]*indexStats.Stats, len(responses))\n\t\tfor i, res := range responses {\n\t\t\tstats[i] = res.(*IndexStatsResponse).Response\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmergedIndexStats := indexStats.MergeStats(stats...)\n\n\t\treturn &IndexStatsResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: &mergedIndexStats,\n\t\t\tHeaders:  headers,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *VolumeResponse:\n\t\tresp0 := responses[0].(*VolumeResponse)\n\t\theaders := resp0.Headers\n\n\t\tresps := make([]*logproto.VolumeResponse, 0, len(responses))\n\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n\t\t\tresps = append(resps, r.(*VolumeResponse).Response)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &VolumeResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: seriesvolume.Merge(resps, resp0.Response.Limit),\n\t\t\tHeaders:  headers,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *DetectedFieldsResponse:\n\t\tresp0 := responses[0].(*DetectedFieldsResponse)\n\t\theaders := resp0.Headers\n\t\tlimit := resp0.Response.GetLimit()\n\n\t\tfields := []*logproto.DetectedField{}\n\t\tvalues := []string{}\n\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n\t\t\tfields = append(fields, r.(*DetectedFieldsResponse).Response.Fields...)\n\t\t\tvalues = append(values, r.(*DetectedFieldsResponse).Response.Values...)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmergedFields, err := detected.MergeFields(fields, limit)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmergedValues, err := detected.MergeValues(values, limit)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &DetectedFieldsResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: &logproto.DetectedFieldsResponse{\n\t\t\t\tFields: mergedFields,\n\t\t\t\tValues: mergedValues,\n\t\t\t\tLimit:  limit,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tHeaders: headers,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tcase *DetectedLabelsResponse:\n\t\tresp0 := responses[0].(*DetectedLabelsResponse)\n\t\theaders := resp0.Headers\n\t\tvar labels []*logproto.DetectedLabel\n\n\t\tfor _, r := range responses {\n\t\t\tlabels = append(labels, r.(*DetectedLabelsResponse).Response.DetectedLabels...)\n\t\t}\n\t\tmergedLabels, err := detected.MergeLabels(labels)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &DetectedLabelsResponse{\n\t\t\tResponse: &logproto.DetectedLabelsResponse{\n\t\t\t\tDetectedLabels: mergedLabels,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t\tHeaders: headers,\n\t\t}, nil\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unknown response type (%T) in merging responses\", responses[0])\n\t}\n}\n\n// mergeOrderedNonOverlappingStreams merges a set of ordered, nonoverlapping responses by concatenating matching streams then running them through a heap to pull out limit values\nfunc mergeOrderedNonOverlappingStreams(resps []*LokiResponse, limit uint32, direction logproto.Direction) []logproto.Stream {\n\tvar total int\n\n\t// turn resps -> map[labels] []entries\n\tgroups := make(map[string]*byDir)\n\tfor _, resp := range resps {\n\t\tfor _, stream := range resp.Data.Result {\n\t\t\ts, ok := groups[stream.Labels]\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\ts = &byDir{\n\t\t\t\t\tdirection: direction,\n\t\t\t\t\tlabels:    stream.Labels,\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tgroups[stream.Labels] = s\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\ts.markers = append(s.markers, stream.Entries)\n\t\t\ttotal += len(stream.Entries)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// optimization: since limit has been reached, no need to append entries from subsequent responses\n\t\tif total >= int(limit) {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tkeys := make([]string, 0, len(groups))\n\tfor key := range groups {\n\t\tkeys = append(keys, key)\n\t}\n\tif direction == logproto.BACKWARD {\n\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse(sort.StringSlice(keys)))\n\t} else {\n\t\tsort.Strings(keys)\n\t}\n\n\t// escape hatch, can just return all the streams\n\tif total <= int(limit) {\n\t\tresults := make([]logproto.Stream, 0, len(keys))\n\t\tfor _, key := range keys {\n\t\t\tresults = append(results, logproto.Stream{\n\t\t\t\tLabels:  key,\n\t\t\t\tEntries: groups[key].merge(),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn results\n\t}\n\n\tpq := &priorityqueue{\n\t\tdirection: direction,\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, key := range keys {\n\t\tstream := &logproto.Stream{\n\t\t\tLabels:  key,\n\t\t\tEntries: groups[key].merge(),\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(stream.Entries) > 0 {\n\t\t\tpq.streams = append(pq.streams, stream)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\theap.Init(pq)\n\n\tresultDict := make(map[string]*logproto.Stream)\n\n\t// we want the min(limit, num_entries)\n\tfor i := 0; i < int(limit) && pq.Len() > 0; i++ {\n\t\t// grab the next entry off the queue. This will be a stream (to preserve labels) with one entry.\n\t\tnext := heap.Pop(pq).(*logproto.Stream)\n\n\t\ts, ok := resultDict[next.Labels]\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\ts = &logproto.Stream{\n\t\t\t\tLabels:  next.Labels,\n\t\t\t\tEntries: make([]logproto.Entry, 0, int(limit)/len(keys)), // allocation hack -- assume uniform distribution across labels\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tresultDict[next.Labels] = s\n\t\t}\n\t\t// TODO: make allocation friendly\n\t\ts.Entries = append(s.Entries, next.Entries...)\n\t}\n\n\tresults := make([]logproto.Stream, 0, len(resultDict))\n\tfor _, key := range keys {\n\t\tstream, ok := resultDict[key]\n\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\tresults = append(results, *stream)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn results\n}\n\nfunc toProtoMatrix(m
